						duration = -1
						hidden = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	
		# Nekheis cheap colonies modifier and event to make them start colonizing
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = G53 #Empkeios
					tag = G58 #Keyolion
					tag = G55 #Eneion
					tag = G54 #Besolaki
					tag = G57 #Apikhoxi
					tag = G59 #Anisikheion
					tag = G56 #Deyeion
					tag = G62 #Amgremos
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = nekheis_cheap_colonies
				duration = 18250 #50 years
			}
			country_event = {
				id = kheionai.200
			}
		}
		if = { #Ameion doesn't need help colonizing so they just get the event
			limit = { tag = G52 } #Ameion
			country_event = { id = kheionai.200 }
		}
		
		# Dwarovar cheap colonies modifier and event to make them start colonizing
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = M01 #Grizehud
					tag = M02 #Dursikari
					tag = H73 #Skewered Drake
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = diggy.759
			}
		}
		
		#Effelai Worship Startup Events
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = chahinanito
				NOT = {
					num_of_cities = 2
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = effelai_worship.2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = tswohvwohii
				NOT = {
					num_of_cities = 2
				}
			}
			country_event = {

on_province_owner_change_effect = {
	on_province_owner_change_government_effect = yes
	on_province_owner_change_estate_privileges_effect = yes
	anb_on_province_owner_change_government_reform_effect = yes
	#Anbennar

	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				is_migratory_tribe = yes
				NOT = { num_of_cities = 2 } # be extra safe - check they're an OPM
			}
			is_empty = yes
			NOT = { has_province_flag = someone_migrated_here_dawg }
		}
		# note this province was migrated out of so the culture change event handles it properly
	
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = majority_setup_complete } }
			}
			# fix edge case - if you migrate immediately without unpausing (after uncolonised but before country setup)
			# the province you migrated out of has no majority
			# only possible if the person migrating has not done majority setup yet, so fix here
			add_majority_of_current_culture = yes	
		} 
	
		set_province_flag = someone_migrated_here_dawg
		#we have the define that clears province flags on becoming unowned AIYEEEE, surely i can set it on uncolonised provinces

		if = { limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = migratory_small_minority } }
			set_province_flag = migratory_small_minority
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = migratory_small_minority }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = migratory_large_minority } }
			set_province_flag = migratory_large_minority
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = migratory_large_minority }
		}
		# oh the clunkiness, transfer the flags from country to province
		# now when the culture update is called, it will save whether there was a small or large minority, so it can be restored later
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				culture_is_mechanim = yes
				is_mechanim_tribe = yes
				NOT = { num_of_cities = 2 } # be extra safe - check they're an OPM
			}
		}
		province_event = { id = mechanim.2 }
	}

	#Krakazol/Rahen initial friendship, formerly rahen.1

on_primary_culture_changed_effect = {

	if = { #Mechanim that hasn't yet unlocked artificery: you get mechanim setup
		limit = { culture_is_mechanim = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_not_banned_magic = yes }
			set_country_flag = banned_magic_via_mechanim
			ban_magic = yes #Ban magic - also closes magic menus
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_institution = manufactories } }
			set_country_flag = artificery_unlocked #Need this first so the scripted event doesn't try to let you choose your org
			artifice_magic_switch_to_artificery_only_mode = yes
			country_event = {
				id = insyaa_flavour.51
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_working_mechanim
			set_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_allowed
		}
	}
	else = {
		clr_country_flag = mechanim_automatory_building_working_mechanim
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = banned_magic_via_mechanim }
			clr_country_flag = banned_magic_via_mechanim
			unban_magic = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = non_artificery_culture #you have the artificery penalty flag
			is_artificery_culture_government = yes #but you shouldn't
		}
		clr_country_flag = non_artificery_culture
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_reform = black_demesne_reform
				has_reform = black_acolyte_reform
			}
			NOT = { primary_culture = black_demesner }
		}
		change_primary_culture = black_demesner
	}

	#Khet mandate opinion modifier for enforcing culture
	if = {
		limit = { 
			is_subject_of_type = tributary_state 
			overlord = { primary_culture = ROOT }
		}
		add_opinion = { who = overlord modifier = khet_forced_culture }
		# Samsumbat (F60) Republicanism reform
		if = {
			limit = {
				empire_of_china_reform_passed = republicanism_steward_reform
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { government = republic }
				}
				change_government = republic
			}
			add_government_reform = republic_of_free_peoples
		}
	}
	#Ynn River Worship Ynnicised culture
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of_type = ynnic_iosahar	#if you are an iosahar
			overlord = {
				primary_culture = ROOT #and your owner converted your culture
				NOT = {
					primary_culture = sarnik
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				overlord = { has_country_modifier = yrw_4b }	#if they got the reform for ynnicising
				NOT = {
					primary_culture = sarnik
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture_is_human = yes
				}
				change_primary_culture = sarnik
				if = {
					limit = {
						fast_ruler_is_human = yes
					}
					set_ruler_culture = sarnik
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						fast_heir_is_human = yes
					}
					set_heir_culture = sarnik
				}
				add_opinion = { who = overlord modifier = ynn_enforced_culture }
			}
			every_owned_province = {	#and you get a culture conversion buff
				limit = {
					OR = {
						culture_is_human = yes 
						culture = horizon_elf
						culture = pipefoot_halfling
						culture = steel_dwarf
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = yrw_assimilate_ynnsmen
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = yrw_enforced_culture	#people get mad
				duration = 10950
			}
			overlord = {
				every_subject_country = {	#very mad
					add_liberty_desire = 10
					add_opinion = {
						who = PREV
						modifier = ynn_enforced_culture
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Reduced gov cap in primary culture
	if = {
		limit = { has_government_attribute = reduced_gov_cost_in_primary_culture }
		every_owned_province = { 
			if = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = cultural_colonies_mod } 
				remove_province_modifier = cultural_colonies_mod
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_owner_culture = yes }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = cultural_colonies_mod
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	assign_dvp_cultural_aspects = yes

	if = {
		limit = { primary_culture = mossmouth_ogre }
		set_country_flag = was_mossmouth_ogre
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = flooded_province
				culture = mossmouth_ogre
			}
			remove_province_modifier = flooded_province
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = flooded_province_inactive duration = -1 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = was_mossmouth_ogre
			NOT = { primary_culture = mossmouth_ogre }
		}
		clr_country_flag = was_mossmouth_ogre
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = flooded_province_inactive }
			remove_province_modifier = flooded_province_inactive
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = flooded_province duration = -1 }
		}
	}

	# Roosts activating/deactivating when you change to/from Harpy culture.
	harpy_roost_se_on_primary_culture_changed_effect = yes

	if = {
		limit = { primary_culture = sunrise_elf }
		set_country_flag = cannot_change_to_elven_military_unless_enough_dev
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_reform = z22_prince_elect
				has_reform = z22_prince_elect_improved
			}
			NOT = {
				culture_is_elven = yes
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = z22_election_cycle_modifier
	}
}

on_scorch_earth_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = I33_clan_of_archers_reward } }
		ROOT = { add_mil_power = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { has_government_mechanic = karakhanbar_flames_of_the_black_hearth_mechanic }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_terrain = ancient_forest }
			ROOT = {
				add_government_power = {
					mechanic_type = karakhanbar_flames_of_the_black_hearth_mechanic
					power_type = karakhanbar_flames_of_the_black_hearth_power
					value = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			ROOT = {
				add_government_power = {
					mechanic_type = karakhanbar_flames_of_the_black_hearth_mechanic
					power_type = karakhanbar_flames_of_the_black_hearth_power
					value = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { has_government_attribute = scorch_earth_slash_and_burn_effect }
			OR = {
				has_terrain = forest
				has_terrain = bloodgroves
				has_terrain = fey_gladeway
				has_terrain = gladeway
				has_terrain = ancient_forest
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = mushroom_forest_terrain
				has_terrain = jungle
			}
			owned_by = ROOT
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = karakhanbar_slash_and_burn
			duration = 1825
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { has_country_flag = karakhanbar_moderates_won }
			owned_by = ROOT
		}
		add_devastation = -5 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { has_country_flag = karakhanbar_hardliners_won }
			NOT = { owned_by = ROOT }
		}
		add_devastation = 10
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = karakhanbar_feyinfused_grove
			controlled_by = ROOT
		}
		remove_province_modifier = karakhanbar_feyinfused_grove
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				tag = S90
			}
		}
		S90 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = S90_scorch_count
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

S53_won_battle_against_trolls = {
	change_variable = {
		trollBattlesWon = 1
	}	
}

anb_on_exploit_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = anb_on_action_tracking_exploit_dev_flag } }
		set_province_flag = anb_has_been_exploited_flag
		add_province_modifier = { name = owner_exploited_$dev$ duration = -1 hidden = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_government_attribute = centaur_refund_exploit_dev }
			has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
		}
		add_base_$dev$ = 1
		add_devastation = 15
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { religion = devouring_path } }
		owner = { add_church_power = 15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = karakhanbar_not_losing_development_chance }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_base_$dev$ = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = wyvernheart_exploit_culture
			}
			has_construction = culture
		}
		add_construction_progress = 0.33
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = B28_ash_flag
				has_reform = B28_rule_of_the_strong
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = B28_looting_province_$dev$
			duration = 3650
			}
		province_event = {
			id = flavour_dogeater.999
			days = 3650
		}
	}
	if = { #Kheionai
		limit = {
			owner = { has_reform = kheionai_the_kheionolyklos }
			has_seat_in_parliament = yes
			NOT = {
				has_terrain = city_terrain
				development = 20
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = kheionai_the_kheionolyklos_good_mod
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = kheionai_the_kheionolyklos_bad_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	giberd_exploit_benonhill = yes
	if_chi_wellspring_reset_size_activity = yes #Transmutative Path
	diggy_diggy_uesrennu = yes
	fires_beneath_exploit_dev = yes
	if = { #umbral covenant
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = S90
					tag = S30
				}
			}
		}
		set_province_flag = S90_exploited_dev
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = S90_exploit_count
				value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = S90_extraction
				}
			}
			S90 = {
				change_mana = {
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #dbco
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_modifier = S30_convert_exploit
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = S30_local_convert
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
	}
	#Eighard
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = H14 } } }
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = eighard_exploit_dev_value
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = H14_hibernal_level_3 }
				H14_hibernal_requisitions_effect = { level = level_three }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = H14_hibernal_level_2 }
				H14_hibernal_requisitions_effect = { level = level_two }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { mission_completed = H14_tap_the_populace }
				H14_hibernal_requisitions_effect = { level = level_one }
			}			
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = H14_consume } }
			add_devastation = -100
			owner = {
				add_church_power = 25
				add_absolutism = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { mission_completed = H14_field_of_broken_oaths }
				NOT = { culture = tuathak }
			}
			add_base_$dev$ = -1
			 if = {
                limit = {
                    owner = { mission_completed = H14_champions_no_longer }
                }
                remove_province_modifier = H14_conversion_efforts
                add_or_extend_province_modifier_effect = {
                    MODIFIER = H14_conversion_efforts_two
                    DURATION = 7300
                }
            }
            else = {
                add_or_extend_province_modifier_effect = {
                    MODIFIER = H14_conversion_efforts
                    DURATION = 7300
                }
            }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = { tag = L76 }
			OR = {
				trade_goods = copper
				trade_goods = iron
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = gashaExploitedDevelopmentCounter
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				owns = 1016
				can_use_sacred_grove_generic_country_reqs_trigger = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = blood_contract_2
					has_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_3
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_2 }
				set_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_3
				clr_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_1 }
				set_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_2
				clr_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_1
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = sacred_grove_exploit_dev_1
			}
		}
	}
}
on_province_owner_change_monuments = {
	##### When monument changes owner #####
	if = { #Ash Palace
		limit = { province_id = 625 }
		FROM = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = golden_highway_v2
			}
		}
		# Take away shared bonuses from any country that is or was Nansaslen.
		if = { limit = { FROM = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = F33 } } }
			random_country = { limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = F80 } }
				remove_country_modifier = F80_cmod_monument_copy_ash_palace_1
				remove_country_modifier = F80_cmod_monument_copy_ash_palace_2
				remove_country_modifier = F80_cmod_monument_copy_ash_palace_3
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #Library of Aqatbar
		limit = { province_id = 536 }
		FROM = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = eduz_ginakku_university
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #PORT JAHER
		limit = { 
			province_id = 365
		}
		FROM = {
			every_owned_province = {
				ascajar_remove_culture_modifier = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = ascajar
					tier = 1
				}
			}
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
							has_owner_culture = yes
						}
					}
					ascajar_accepted_culture_modifier = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { province_id = 5808 } #Dendugma Monastery
		FROM = {
			every_owned_province = {
				dendugma_monastery_remove_modifier = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				A02 = {
					mission_completed = deranne_tremendous_firepower
				}
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = A02
						is_subject_of = A02
					}
				}
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = A02
							is_subject_of = A02
						}
					}
				}
			}
			A02 = {
				remove_country_modifier = deranne_dendugma_monastery_modifier_1
				remove_country_modifier = deranne_dendugma_monastery_modifier_2
				remove_country_modifier = deranne_dendugma_monastery_modifier_3
				every_owned_province = {
					dendugma_monastery_remove_modifier = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_great_project = {
					type = dendugma_monastery
					tier = 2
				}
			}
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = ironwood_trees
					}
					dendugma_monastery_ironwood_modifier = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					A02 = { mission_completed = deranne_tremendous_firepower }
					owner = { 
						is_subject_of = A02
					}
				}
				A02 = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = ironwood_trees
						}
						dendugma_monastery_ironwood_modifier = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { province_id = 6632 } #Lizardfolk Port
		if = {
			limit = {
				A02 = {
					has_country_flag = deranne_completed_teramzadai_quest
				}
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = A02
					}
				}
			}
			A02 = {
				remove_country_modifier = deranne_lizardport_upgrade_modifier_1
				remove_country_modifier = deranne_lizardport_upgrade_modifier_2
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #Grave Forest of Ilvandet
		limit = { province_id = 31 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				grave_forest_of_ilvandet_is_active = yes
				has_great_project = { type = grave_forest_of_ilvandet tier = 1 }
			}
			if = { #stricly level one
				limit = { NOT = { has_great_project = { type = grave_forest_of_ilvandet tier = 2 } } }
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = { OR = { region = lencenor_region region = west_dameshead_region } has_terrain = ancient_forest }
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = grave_forest_expanded_infrastructure
							duration = -1
							hidden = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #level two
				limit = { NOT = { has_great_project = { type = grave_forest_of_ilvandet tier = 3 } } }
				owner = { 
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							OR = { region = lencenor_region region = west_dameshead_region }
							OR = {
								has_terrain = forest
								has_terrain = woods
								has_terrain = ancient_forest
							}
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = grave_forest_expanded_infrastructure
							duration = -1
							hidden = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #level three
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							OR = { region = lencenor_region region = west_dameshead_region }
							OR = {
								has_terrain = forest
								has_terrain = woods
								has_terrain = ancient_forest
							}
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = grave_forest_expanded_infrastructure
							duration = -1
							hidden = yes
						}
					}
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_terrain = forest
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = grave_forest_forest
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_terrain = woods
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = grave_forest_wood
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_terrain = ancient_forest
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = grave_forest_ancient_forest
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { #remove from prev owner
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = grave_forest_expanded_infrastructure
				remove_province_modifier = grave_forest_forest
				remove_province_modifier = grave_forest_wood
				remove_province_modifier = grave_forest_ancient_forest
			}
			clr_country_flag = unlocked_privilege_estate_burghers_forest_expansion
		}
	}
	if = { #Imperial Palace
		limit = {
			province_id = 8
		}
		every_country = {
			remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_1
			remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_2
			remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_3
		}
		emperor = {

		limit = {
			province_id = 4630 #Sarilavhan
			has_construction = iron_palace
			NOT = {
				is_capital = yes
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = iron_seal_found
					owned_by = R00 
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_construction = yes #hidden construction bug
		#if you annex your subject while they are upgrading the monument, it continues but is hidden
		#the iron_palace construction is really long and you can't speed it up with this bug, so cancel it here
	}
	##Temple of Ruby and Bronze
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				owns = 5774
			}
			5774 = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = temple_ruby_bronze
					tier = 2
				}
				sarhal_owner_can_use_temple_ruby_bronze = yes
			}
			OR = {
				trade_goods = grain
				trade_goods = livestock
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				5774 = {
					has_great_project = {
						type = temple_ruby_bronze
						tier = 3
					}
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = temple_of_ruby_and_bronze_livestock_mod_2
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = temple_of_ruby_and_bronze_livestock_mod_1
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	##Garden of Perpetual Change
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = bustebe_dajadera_tier_2_mod
		}
		remove_province_modifier = bustebe_dajadera_tier_2_mod
		FROM = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
				}
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = bustebe_dajadera_tier_2_mod
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = bustebe_dajadera_tier_3_mod
		}
		remove_province_modifier = bustebe_dajadera_tier_3_mod
		FROM = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
				}
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = bustebe_dajadera_tier_3_mod
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Imzeri - the Blackstone City
	if = { #If owns the monument and can use it - add the modifier
		limit = {
			owner = {
				owns = 5631
				can_use_izmeri_the_black_stone_city = yes
			}
			5631 = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = izmeri_the_black_stone_city
					tier = 2
				}
			}
			has_coast_defense_building_trigger = yes
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = izmeri_expand_the_buildings }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = izmeri_expand_the_buildings
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	#Mewomender - Holy Triplets of Mewomender
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner_has_active_triplets_tier_3 = yes
		}
		triplets_add_development_effect = yes
	}
	#Iochand
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				province_id = 66
				province_id = 63
				province_id = 112
				province_id = 70
				province_id = 86
				province_id = 190
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					overlord = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = A80 } }
					is_subject_of_type = hezoggdoum
				}
			}
			owner = { overlord = { iochand_hezoggdoum_owned_monument_effect_all = yes } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					overlord = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = A80 } }
					is_subject_of_type = hezoggdoum
				}
			}
			FROM = { overlord = { iochand_hezoggdoum_owned_monument_effect_all = yes } }
		}
	}

	# Secret of the Hinuilands
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = hinuilands_secret_here
		}
		province_event = { id = insyaa_flavour.2003 } #on_secret_of_the_hinuilands_owned needs a 1 day delay
	}
	
	hinuibee_hive_province_owner_change = yes
	fluvial_waterworks_province_owner_change = yes
}

on_production_manufactory_built_effect = { #Farm Estate, Wharf, Plantation but not Ramparts
	owner = { accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = tea_ceremonies category = dip amount = 25 } }
	owner = {
		#Molten Eternity
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = infinite_self_generosity
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = 100
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { tag_allowed_dragon_turtle_system = yes }
			province_with_arable_goods = yes
		}
		owner = { dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = grandfather_moss amount = 3 } }
	}
}

on_production_manufactory_destroyed_effect = { #Farm Estate, Wharf, Plantation but not Ramparts
	owner = {
		#Molten Eternity
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = infinite_self_generosity
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = -100
			}
		}
	}
}

on_idea_taken_effect = { #Any basic idea e.g. "War Council" in Mercenary ideas or "Global Empire" in Exploration
	accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = peacock_emissaries category = dip amount = 40 }
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = molten_eternity
			has_personal_deity = speaking_memory_responsibility
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moltenEternityObligationVar
			value = 200
		}
	}
}

on_idea_removed_effect = { #When any basic idea is removed

}

on_idea_group_finished_effect = { #Taking the final idea in an idea group i.e. the seventh idea
	increase_legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod = yes
}

on_idea_group_unfinished_effect = { #Removing the final idea in a group whereas it had previously been completed
	decrease_legitimacy_equivalent_absolutism_from_idea_groups_mod = yes
}

on_consort_death_effects = {
	country_event = { id = flavour_covenblad.80 } # Covenblad Palatine Arbiter stuff
	country_event = { id = flavor_averilibet.3 } #averilibet husband harem 
	country_event = { id = flavor_frozenmaw.14 } #the death of Frida
	country_event = { id = guwaamud.100 } # Harem lady dead
	country_event = { id = flavour_lelanan.81 } #Death of Leli and Felana
	magic_on_consort_death = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_consort_flag = 10_years_anniversary }
		set_ruler_flag = had_10_years_anniversary
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_consort_flag = 20_years_anniversary }
		set_ruler_flag = had_20_years_anniversary
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_consort_flag = consort_has_affection_of_ruler }
		set_ruler_flag = consort_had_affection_of_ruler
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_regency = no
			NOT = { has_ruler_flag = widow_widower }
		}
		set_ruler_flag = widow_widower
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_consort_regency = no }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = domain_of_spouses_family }
			remove_province_modifier = domain_of_spouses_family
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = accepted_help_from_spouses_family }
		clr_ruler_flag = accepted_help_from_spouses_family
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = helped_spouses_family }
		clr_ruler_flag = helped_spouses_family
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = refused_to_help_spouses_family }
		clr_ruler_flag = refused_to_help_spouses_family
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = has_lowborn_consort }
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = home_of_consort }
			remove_province_modifier = home_of_consort
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = has_lowborn_consort }
		clr_ruler_flag = has_lowborn_consort
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = consort_adm_advice }
		remove_country_modifier = consort_adm_advice
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = consort_dip_advice }
		remove_country_modifier = consort_dip_advice
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = consort_mil_advice }
		remove_country_modifier = consort_mil_advice
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = without_spouse_advice }
		remove_country_modifier = without_spouse_advice
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_modifier = affectionate_royal_couple }
		remove_country_modifier = affectionate_royal_couple
	}

	#Duwarkani consorts
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = duwarkani_admin_consort
		}
		remove_country_modifier = duwarkani_admin_consort
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = duwarkani_diplo_consort
		}
		remove_country_modifier = duwarkani_diplo_consort
	}

		remove_country_modifier = duwarkani_mil_consort

	clr_ruler_flag = marriage_length
